<span>Honest review after using for 1 month</span>
</a></div><span class="a-size-base a-color-secondary review-date" data-hook="review-date">Reviewed in India  on 18 November 2020</span><div class="a-row a-spacing-mini review-data review-format-strip"><span class="a-declarative" data-action="reviews:filter-action:push-state" data-csa-c-func-deps="aui-da-reviews:filter-action:push-state" data-csa-c-type="widget" data-reviews:filter-action:push-state="{}"><a class="a-link-normal" data-reftag="cm_cr_arp_d_rvw_rvwer" data-reviews-state-param='{"pageNumber":"1","reviewerType":"avp_only_reviews"}' href="/Apple-iPhone-11-64GB-Green/product-reviews/B07XVKBY68?reviewerType=avp_only_reviews"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold" data-hook="avp-badge">Verified Purchase</span></a></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small review-data"><span class="a-size-base review-text review-text-content" data-hook="review-body">
<span>I am writing this review exactly after using this product for 1 month. I was skeptical after reading so many negative reviews for this phone but still took a chance to buy. I received the product the very next day with perfect packaging and everything intact. Purchased this product for around 46k after receiving debit card discount. Unboxed it and there was this premium looking phone. I have received all the accessories and a brand new product.<br/>I was an android user for past 11 years so using this product was an entirely different experience.<br/><br/>Pros:<br/>1. Superb processor-  My iphone has not hanged a single time while using regressively. 10+ apps are opened at once still it was buttery smooth<br/>2. Amazing camera- The night mode feature of the camera seal the deal with good potrait mode<br/>3. Battery lasting for a day- I have always heard from my friends that iPhone doesn't have a good battery back up but this model is lasting for a day which is sufficient<br/>4. No heating issue- I have not faced any heating issue till date<br/>5. Security- The phone has good features for securing the data and doesn't have unnecessary applications<br/><br/>Cons:<br/>1. Charger- The charger provided with this phone is just not sufficient. It takes 3 hours to charge my phone<br/>2. No 3.5mm jack- It doesn't have a designated port for connecting your normal headphones. You have to buy expensive jack of 900rs from apple stores<br/>3. Slo mo video- The slo mo videos created on the phone creates distorted image and feels like it has been taken by a 2 year old child who cannot hold the phone still.<br/>4. Customisation- An android user knows how easy it is to customize their phone according to their preference. You can customise a little on iphone but it is very limited.<br/>5. Expensive- iPhone which costs around 50k also needs accessories which are expensive like fast charger for around 1900rs, 3.5mm lightening jack 900rs, icloud storage 75rs/month, apple care etc.<br/><br/>Overall I am really impressed with the product and these cons can somewhat be neglected if you're an iPhone user for a long time.</span>
</span></div><div class="a-popover-preload" id="a-popover-R2N8KF37KYNR4P_gallerySection_main">
<div class="a-section cr-lightbox-popover-container" data-hook="image-popover" id="R2N8KF37KYNR4P_image_popover">

<div class="a-section a-spacing-mini cr-review-stars-and-title">
<i class="a-icon a-icon-star a-star-5 cr-lightbox-review-rating"><span class="a-icon-alt">5.0 out of 5 stars</span></i>
<span class="a-size-base cr-lightbox-review-title a-text-bold">
                Honest review after using for 1 month
            </span>
<br/>
<span class="a-size-small a-color-secondary cr-lightbox-review-origin">
                
                    
                    
                        
                            
                                By Sanya on 18 November 2020
                            
                            
                        
                    
                
            </span>
</div>
<span class="a-size-base cr-lightbox-review-body">
            I am writing this review exactly after using this product for 1 month. I was skeptical after reading so many negative reviews for this phone but still took a chance to buy. I received the product the very next day with perfect packaging and everything intact. Purchased this product for around 46k after receiving debit card discount. Unboxed it and there was this premium looking phone. I have received all the accessories and a brand new product.<br>I was an android user for past 11 years so using this product was an entirely different experience.<br/><br/>Pros:<br/>1. Superb processor-  My iphone has not hanged a single time while using regressively. 10+ apps are opened at once still it was buttery smooth<br/>2. Amazing camera- The night mode feature of the camera seal the deal with good potrait mode<br/>3. Battery lasting for a day- I have always heard from my friends that iPhone doesn't have a good battery back up but this model is lasting for a day which is sufficient<br/>4. No heating issue- I have not faced any heating issue till date<br/>5. Security- The phone has good features for securing the data and doesn't have unnecessary applications<br/><br/>Cons:<br/>1. Charger- The charger provided with this phone is just not sufficient. It takes 3 hours to charge my phone<br/>2. No 3.5mm jack- It doesn't have a designated port for connecting your normal headphones. You have to buy expensive jack of 900rs from apple stores<br/>3. Slo mo video- The slo mo videos created on the phone creates distorted image and feels like it has been taken by a 2 year old child who cannot hold the phone still.<br/>4. Customisation- An android user knows how easy it is to customize their phone according to their preference. You can customise a little on iphone but it is very limited.<br/>5. Expensive- iPhone which costs around 50k also needs accessories which are expensive like fast charger for around 1900rs, 3.5mm lightening jack 900rs, icloud storage 75rs/month, apple care etc.<br/><br/>Overall I am really impressed with the product and these cons can somewhat be neglected if you're an iPhone user for a long time.
        </br></span>

<span>Love iPhone</span>
</a></div><span class="a-size-base a-color-secondary review-date" data-hook="review-date">Reviewed in India  on 1 February 2022</span><div class="a-row a-spacing-mini review-data review-format-strip"><span class="a-declarative" data-action="reviews:filter-action:push-state" data-csa-c-func-deps="aui-da-reviews:filter-action:push-state" data-csa-c-type="widget" data-reviews:filter-action:push-state="{}"><a class="a-link-normal" data-reftag="cm_cr_arp_d_rvw_rvwer" data-reviews-state-param='{"pageNumber":"1","reviewerType":"avp_only_reviews"}' href="/Apple-iPhone-11-64GB-Green/product-reviews/B07XVKBY68?reviewerType=avp_only_reviews"><span class="a-size-mini a-color-state a-text-bold" data-hook="avp-badge">Verified Purchase</span></a></span></div><div class="a-row a-spacing-small review-data"><span class="a-size-base review-text review-text-content" data-hook="review-body">
<span>I had been using Android mobiles before iPhone 11, after using my iPhone 11, I felt very bad that I wasted my time and money on Android phones.<br/><br/>Reason to change from Android to iPhone - Privacy, security and few ads that were shown on Android were shocking, that time I felt like I should move away from Android.<br/><br/>Why I Love iPhone?<br/>1) Easy navigation, it understands humans very well, it exactly does what we want to do / act next. amazing.<br/>2) 100% Privacy and security. I can kept my iphone at any place in my home or office, no one can see my messages / whatapp popups etc. Feeling relaxed.<br/>3) Good Camera,  equivalent to professional Canon/ Sony cameras. Half of my professional photography and video work is done on iPhone. It saves money too.<br/>4) Good battery life, User friendly system.<br/>5) Super fast system.</span>

<script type="text/javascript">(function ($Nav) {
"use strict";

if (typeof $Nav === 'undefined' || $Nav === null || typeof $Nav.when !== 'function') {
    return;
}

$Nav.when('$', 'data', 'flyout.yourAccount', 'sidepanel.csYourAccount',
          'config')
    .run("BuyitAgain-YourAccount-SidePanel",
    function ($, data, yaFlyout, csYourAccount, config) {
        if (config.disableBuyItAgain) {
            return;
        }
        var render = function (data) {
            if (data.dramResult) {
                var widgetHtml = data.dramResult;
                navbar.sidePanel({
                    flyoutName: 'yourAccount',
                    data: {html: widgetHtml}
                });
            }
        };

        var renderBuyItAgain = function (biaData) {
            if (csYourAccount) {
                csYourAccount.register(render, biaData);
            } else {
                render(biaData);
            }
        };

        yaFlyout.sidePanel.onData(function() {
            if (window.P) {
                P.when('A', 'a-truncate').execute(function(A, truncate) {
                    var truncateElements = A.$('.a-truncate');
                    A.each(truncateElements, function(element) {
                        truncate.get(element).update();
                    });
                    var recommendationsWidget = document.getElementById('bia-hcb-widget');
                    if (recommendationsWidget) { 
                        var navFlyout = recommendationsWidget.parentElement;
                        var navFlyoutPaddingBottom = parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(navFlyout).getPropertyValue('padding-bottom'));
                        var navFlyoutContentHeight = navFlyout.clientHeight - navFlyoutPaddingBottom;
                        while (recommendationsWidget.offsetHeight > navFlyoutContentHeight){
                            var recommendations = recommendationsWidget.querySelectorAll('.biaNavFlyoutFaceout');
                            if (recommendations.length <= 1) {
                                break;
                            }
                            var lastRecommendation = recommendations[recommendations.length - 1];
                            lastRecommendation.parentElement.removeChild(lastRecommendation);
                        }
                    }
               });
            }
        });

    yaFlyout.onRender(function() {
            $.ajax({
                url: '/gp/bia/external/bia-hcb-ajax-handler.html',
                data: {"biaHcbRid":"0QBVEZJM0GAB991JSGSF"},
                dataType: 'json',
                timeout: 4*1000,
                success: renderBuyItAgain,
                error: function (jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                }
            });
        });
    });
})(window.$Nav);</script>

      [<span class="a-size-base review-text review-text-content" data-hook="review-body">
 <span>Well well well! The most hyped iPhone of the year isnt quite there at least not for me.<br/>It has a best camera undoubtedly, but the other side of the coin is not that good. So I was an android user, 1 Plus more specifically. I was excited to switch to the iPhone as most of you maybe. Amazon was pretty good at the delivery and I got it within 3 days. During my first day usage I noticed a slight warm feeling on the right side of my phone from top to bottom on the back. It was prominent and I could feel the heat that was generated. I looked online and fixed some setting like location and notifications which would put a lot of pressure on your battery. So i thought it is fixed but it wasnt.<br/>To be honest I never thought of iPhones getting warm within a few minutes of youtube playback or social networking on WhatsApp or Instagram. It was all that I had never thought of. My onePlus 6 was a beast in this matter and half the price of iPhone 11, nonetheless I used it for a few days and kept looking for solutions but all would say it is quite normal for an iPhone to get warm.<br/>To be on the safer side I thought of replacement but Amazon wont allow you unless you have a job sheet from an authorised apple service centre, which was quite new for me. As earlier no matter the cost of the product a replacement window was always open. A disappointment then!<br/>So with a heavy heart I headed towards the iPhone Service Centre some 15 kms away from my place. While reaching there I put forward my issues and they were like sir it is quite normal for the iPhones unless you get a warning of over heating. They were not ready to make a job sheet instead suggested for a diagnostic test, which came out normal.<br/>It has been a week now, I can still feel that warmth on the right side of my phone and I suppose I have to get used to it.<br/>Talking about the other things the phone offers, Camera quality is the best, you get some awesome video and audio quality. A top notch I must say.<br/>You will have to cautiously use it for a longer battery life.<br/>The charging brick is good for a normal user, it is a bit slow in charging but it is not necessary to spend some 3000 plus fo a new charger and a cable.<br/>Face recognition is fast but I still miss my fingerprint in times of this Pandemic.<br/>So the bottom line is worst Amazon Experience, you better buy it from an authorised dealer or go to appleonlinestoreindia for some good deals.<br/>And yeah! winter is coming so I have got it covered thanks to iPhone 11:) Cheers!!!</span>

So I was an android user, 1 Plus more specifically. I was excited to switch to the iPhone as most of you maybe. Amazon was pretty good at the delivery and I got it within 3 days. I looked online and fixed some setting like location and notifications which would put a lot of pressure on your battery. It was all that I had never thought of. As earlier no matter the cost of the product a replacement window was always open. A disappointment then!So with a heavy heart I headed towards the iPhone Service Centre some 15 kms away from my place.
